
international_arms_market_category = {
turn_off_ai_usage = {
        available = {
        }
       visible = {
        NOT = { has_global_flag = no_ai_purchase }
        }
        icon = category_generic
        cost = 0
        complete_effect = {
            set_global_flag = no_ai_purchase 
        }
    }
turn_on_ai_usage = {
        available = {
        }
       visible = {
        has_global_flag = no_ai_purchase
        }
        icon = category_generic
        cost = 0
        complete_effect = {
            clr_global_flag = no_ai_purchase 
        }
    }
####support
open_support_menu = {
        available = {
        }
       visible = {
        NOT = { has_country_flag = open_support_menu }
        }
        ai_will_do = {
            factor = 10
            modifier = {
                has_global_flag = no_ai_purchases
                }
                factor = 0
            }
        icon = generic_construction
        cost = 0
        complete_effect = {
            set_country_flag = open_support_menu 
        }
        remove_effect = {
        }
    }
close_support_menu = {
        available = {
        }
       visible = {
        has_country_flag = open_support_menu 
        }
        icon = generic_construction
        cost = 0
        complete_effect = {
            clr_country_flag = open_support_menu 
        }
        remove_effect = {
        }
    }

####SUPPORT
purchase_foreign_trains = {
        available = {
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 1
        }
        days_remove = 90
        visible = {
        has_country_flag = open_support_menu
        }
        icon = decision_category_border_war
        cost = 20

        complete_effect = {
            add_tech_bonus = {
                bonus = 0.5
                uses = 1
                category = train_tech
            }   
        }
        remove_effect = {
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                type = train_equipment_1
                amount = 15
                producer = USA
            }
        }
    }
purchase_english_trucks = {
        available = {
        NOT = { ENG = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            ENG = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
                ENG = {
                    has_opinion = {
                    target = ROOT
                    value > 19
                    }
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2
        }
        days_remove = 90
        visible = {
        ENG = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
        has_country_flag = open_support_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = ENG
            }
            ENG = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = ENG
            }
            country_exists = ENG
        }
        icon = generic_factory
        cost = 20

        complete_effect = {
            ENG = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 2
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = ENG
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = ENG
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                type = motorized_equipment_1
                amount = 120
                producer = ENG
            }

            ENG = {
                add_political_power = 20
            }

            ENG = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = -2
                }
            }
        }
    }

####################################################################################rifles
purchase_american_rifles = {
        available = {
        USA = { 
            any_state = {
            is_capital = YES
            is_owned_and_controlled_by = USA
        }
        }
        NOT = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            USA  = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
                USA = {
                    has_opinion = {
                    target = ROOT
                    value > 9
                    }
                    #has_tech = 
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2
        }
        ai_will_do = {
            factor = 0.1
            modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    num_of_civilian_factories < 10
                    stockpile_ratio = { 
                        archetype = infantry_equipment
                        ratio > 0.75
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        days_remove = 90
        visible = {
        USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            has_country_flag = open_rifle_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = USA
            }
             USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = USA
            }
            country_exists = USA
        }
        icon = generic_industry
        cost = 20

        complete_effect = {
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 2
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {

            USA = {
                add_political_power = 20
            }

            add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                type = infantry_equipment
                amount = 2000
                producer = USA
            }
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = -2
                }
            }
        }
    }


purchase_english_rifles = {
        available = {
        NOT = { ENG = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            ENG = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
                ENG = {
                    has_opinion = {
                    target = ROOT
                    value > 9
                    }
                    #has_tech = 
                }
        }
        ai_will_do = {
            factor = 0.1
            modifier = {
                OR = {
                    num_of_civilian_factories < 5
                    stockpile_ratio = { 
                        archetype = infantry_equipment
                        ratio > 3
                    }
                }
                factor = 0
            }
            modifier = {
                has_war = yes
                factor = 10
            }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2
        }
        days_remove = 90
        visible = {
        ENG = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
                    has_country_flag = open_rifle_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = ENG
            }
            ENG = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = ENG
            }
            country_exists = ENG
        }
        icon = generic_industry

                                ship_anti_air_upgrade = 0
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    create_ship = { type = destroyer_1 equipment_variant = "Surplus Destroyer" creator = ROOT }
                    create_ship = { type = destroyer_1 equipment_variant = "Surplus Destroyer" creator = ROOT }
                }
            }

purchase_american_artillery_pieces = {
        available = {
        NOT = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            USA = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
            USA = {
                has_opinion = {
                    target = ROOT
                    value > 19
                }
            num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
            }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2
        }
        ai_will_do = {
            factor = 0.1
            modifier = {
                OR = {
                    num_of_civilian_factories < 5
                    stockpile_ratio = { 
                        archetype = artillery_equipment
                        ratio > 3
                    }
                }
                factor = 0
            }
            modifier = {
                has_war = yes
                factor = 10
            }
        }
        days_remove = 120
        visible = {
            has_country_flag = open_arty_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = USA
            }
             USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            #        USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = USA
            }
            country_exists = USA
        }
        icon = ger_military_buildup
        cost = 20
        complete_effect = {
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 2
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {

            USA = {
                add_political_power = 20
            }

            add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
                type = artillery_equipment
                amount = 72
                producer = USA
            }
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = -2
                }
            }
        }
    }

                tag = USA

                modifier = BUL_sold_guns

purchase_american_tanks = {
        available = {
        USA = { surrender_progress < 0.9 }
        NOT = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            USA = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 2 
                USA = {
                   has_opinion = {
                        target = ROOT
                        value > 19
                    }
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            #civilian_factory_use = 3

        }
        days_remove = 125
        visible = {
        USA = { 
            NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }
        #has_tech = main_battle_tank 

        }
        has_country_flag = open_tank_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = USA
            }
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = USA
            }
            country_exists = USA
        }
        icon = generic_tank
        cost = 35
        complete_effect = {
            USA = {
                country_event = { id = armsmarket.1 }
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
        }
    }

    purchase_american_medium_tanks = {
        available = {
        NOT = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            USA = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3 
                USA = {
                    has_opinion = {
                        target = ROOT
                        value > 19
                    }
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2

        }
        days_remove = 150
        visible = {

        USA = { 
            OR = {
                has_tech = improved_medium_tank
                has_tech = improved_medium_tank_chassis
            }        
         } 
        has_country_flag = open_tank_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = USA
            }
             USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = USA
            }
            country_exists = USA
        }
        icon = generic_tank
        cost = 30
        complete_effect = {
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 3
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
        IF = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
            }
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
                type = medium_tank_equipment_2
                amount = 100
                producer = USA
            }
        }
        else = {
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
                type = medium_tank_chassis
                amount = 100
                producer = USA
            }
        }

            USA = {
                add_political_power = 30
            }

            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = -2
                }
            }
        }
    }

    purchase_american_heavy_tanks = {
        available = {
        NOT = { USA = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            USA = {
        OR = {
            has_war = no
            has_war_together_with = ROOT
        }
    }
                num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3 
                USA = {
                    has_opinion = {
                        target = ROOT
                        value > 19
                    }
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2

        }
        days_remove = 200
        visible = {
        USA = { 
            NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }
            OR = {
                has_tech = improved_heavy_tank
                has_tech = basic_heavy_tank_chassis
            }   

        }
        has_country_flag = open_tank_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = USA
            }
             USA = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = USA
            }
            country_exists = USA
        }
        icon = generic_tank
        cost = 35
        complete_effect = {
            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 3
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = USA
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
        IF = {
            limit = {
                NOT = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
            }
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
                type = heavy_tank_equipment_2
                amount = 60
                producer = USA
            }
        }
        else = {
            add_equipment_to_stockpile = { 
                type = heavy_tank_chassis
                amount = 60
                producer = USA
            }
        }
            USA = {
                add_political_power = 35
            }

            USA = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = -2
                }
            }
        }
    }

    purchase_an_english_cruiser = {
        available = {
        NOT = { ENG = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
        NOT = { ROOT = { has_idea = closed_economy }}
            ENG = {
                OR = {
                    has_war = no
                    has_war_together_with = ROOT
                }
            }
        num_of_civilian_factories_available_for_projects > 3 
                ENG = {
                    has_opinion = {
                        target = ROOT
                        value > 19
                    }
                }
        }
        modifier = {
            civilian_factory_use = 2
        }
        days_remove = 300
        visible = {
        has_country_flag = open_ship_menu
            NOT = { 
                tag = ENG
            }
            ENG = { NOT = { has_capitulated = yes }}
            NOT = { 
                has_war_with = ENG
            }
            country_exists = ENG
        }
        icon = category_spr_carlism
        cost = 30
        complete_effect = {
            ENG = {
                add_offsite_building = {
                    type = industrial_complex
                    level = 3
                }
                add_opinion_modifier = {
                    target = ROOT
                    modifier = BUL_bought_guns
                }

            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = ENG
                modifier = BUL_sold_guns
            }
            add_opinion_modifier = {
                target = ENG
                modifier = BUL_arms_trade
            }
        }
        remove_effect = {
                        if = {
                limit = { has_dlc = "Man the Guns" }
                if = { 
                    limit = {
                        ENG = { has_tech = advanced_ship_hull_cruiser }
                    }
                    hidden_effect = { add_manpower = 1400 }
                    ENG = {
                        create_equipment_variant = {
                            name = "English Cruiser Purchase"    
                            type = ship_hull_cruiser_4
                            name_group = POR_CL_HISTORICAL
                            parent_version = 0
                            modules = {
                                fixed_ship_battery_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_2

                                rear_1_custom_slot = ship_light_medium_battery_2
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    create_ship = { type = ship_hull_cruiser_4 equipment_variant = "English Cruiser Purchase" creator = ENG }
                }
                else_if = { 
                    limit = {
                        ENG = { has_tech = improved_ship_hull_cruiser }
                    }
                    hidden_effect = { add_manpower = 1200 }
                    ENG = {
                        create_equipment_variant = {
                            name = "English Cruiser Purchase"    
                            type = ship_hull_cruiser_3
                            name_group = POR_CL_HISTORICAL
